< 196:"A Great Rune of the shardbearer Malenia.\nThe blessing of this half-rotted rune reduces the healing power of Flask of Crimson Tears.\n\nAnd yet, due to the infusion of Malenia's spirit of resistance, attacks made immediately after receiving damage will partially recover HP.\n\nMalenia is daughter to Queen Marika and Radagon, and her Great Rune should have been the most sacred of all."

> 210001:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon three winged misbegotten spirits.\n\nSpirits with the aspect of wings which takes flight to loose arrows from its bow. The misbegotten are held to be a punishment for making contact with the Crucible, and from birth they are treated as slaves, or worse."
- 210001:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤带翼混种的灵魂。\n\n拥有翅膀百相，边飞边射箭的灵魂。\n混种的诞生，据说是接触熔炉所降下的惩罚。\n因此他们生来就是奴隶，被称为玷污者。"
= 210001:""

< 235000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirit of a rotten stray.\n\nSpirit of a stray dog corrupted by the scarlet rot.\nThough it is only a small creature, it is as violent as it is nimble, and its fangs fester with poisonous rot."
> 235000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon two rotten stray spirits.\n\nSpirits of stray dogs corrupted by the scarlet rot.\nThough they are only small creatures, they are as violent as they are nimble, and their fangs fester with poisonous rot."
- 235000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤腐败野狗的灵魂。\n\n受到猩红腐败侵蚀的野狗灵魂。\n体型偏小，动作迅速，性格十分凶暴。\n那口骯脏的牙布满了腐败的毒素。"

< 241000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirit of a noble sorcerer.\n\nSpirit of a nobleman who once asked to be given a place at Raya Lucaria to learn glintstone sorceries.\nHis talents were insufficient to be worthy of donning the stone crown, however, and he is only capable of using the most rudimentary sorcery."
> 241000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon three noble sorcerer spirits.\n\nSpirits of noblemen who once asked to be given a place at Raya Lucaria to learn glintstone sorceries.\nTheir talents were insufficient to be worthy of donning the stone crown, however, and they are only capable of using the most rudimentary sorcery."
- 241000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤权贵魔法师的灵魂。\n\n在过去，前往雷亚卢卡利亚魔法学院\n学习辉石魔法的权贵灵魂。\n然而他的资质不足以戴上辉石头罩，\n只能施展非常初阶的魔法。"

> 241006:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon three noble sorcerer spirits.\n\nSpirits of noblemen who once asked to be given a place at Raya Lucaria to learn glintstone sorceries.\nTheir talents were insufficient to be worthy of donning the stone crown, however, and they are only capable of using the most rudimentary sorcery."
- 241006:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤权贵魔法师的灵魂。\n\n在过去，前往雷亚卢卡利亚魔法学院\n学习辉石魔法的权贵灵魂。\n然而他的资质不足以戴上辉石头罩，\n只能施展非常初阶的魔法。"

< 246000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of three little living jars.\nSummoning consumes HP rather than FP.\n\nThese reckless spirits sacrifice themselves to vanquish their summoner's foes, and explode upon death.\nThough their bravery is admirable, their explosions can harm friend as well as foe, and they will also immediately explode on contact with fire.\n\n\"Tell the others—tell them how brightly a fire jar burns.\""
> 246000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of three little living jars.\n\nThese reckless spirits sacrifice themselves to vanquish their summoner's foes, and explode upon death.\nThough their bravery is admirable, their explosions can harm friend as well as foe, and they will also immediately explode on contact with fire.\n\n\"Tell the others—tell them how brightly a fire jar burns.\""
- 246000:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤３名小型活壶的灵魂。\n召唤时不消耗专注值，而是血量。\n\n会对敌人展开特攻，死亡时会爆炸，\n一群视死如归的灵魂。\n表现得很勇敢，但爆炸也会波及我方。\n碰触到火焰会立刻爆炸。\n\n\u3000帮我们转告给故乡的大家吧──\n\u3000我们火焰壶，表现的点点滴滴……"

- 246006:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤３名小型活壶的灵魂。\n召唤时不消耗专注值，而是血量。\n\n会对敌人展开特攻，死亡时会爆炸，\n一群视死如归的灵魂。\n表现得很勇敢，但爆炸也会波及我方。\n碰触到火焰会立刻爆炸。\n\n\u3000帮我们转告给故乡的大家吧──\n\u3000我们火焰壶，表现的点点滴滴……"
